
                                (function() {
                                    const theme = document.cookie.split('; ').find(row => row.startsWith('docsColorTheme='));
                                    if (theme) {
                                        document.body.className = theme.split('=')[1] + "Theme";
                                    }
                                })();

## [](#February%2024,%202026)February 24, 20262026年2月24日

### [](#February%2024,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#f7a0a878fb722d7bb4a62fddd1710f4eb34b21ee864903e0563b177741c5c96b)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now includes a trash icon in its toolbar that enables you to remove trashed resources from your graph and exclude them from node connections. This allows you to focus on active resources and simplifies navigation, especially when working with complex workflows containing many nodes. You can add the trashed resources back to your graph by selecting the trash icon again.

![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-02-18-13-50-26-filter-trashed-resources.png](2026-02-18-13-50-26-filter-trashed-resources.png)

## [](#February%2023,%202026)February 23, 20262026年2月23日

### [](#February%2023,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#0d0a193a79cd7319a116e5c7da6a8a301f3048c6192f5b566e439753c2c48ee0)[Ontology / Machinery](/docs/foundry/process-mining/)You can now open Machinery processes in Workflow Lineage directly from the Machinery application. Access this functionality through the new **Open in Workflow Lineage** option in the **File** menu dropdown, or by using the keyboard shortcut `ctrl + i` (Windows) or `cmd + i` (macOS).
- [](#3d1bdf5199e2498a845062197b256eacf2f265b77544e47bd3c457cf20373ddd)[Ontology / Ontology Management](/docs/foundry/ontology-manager/)Ontology Manager now supports creating materializations for object types. This feature allows you to define how object data should be materialized. Currently, this functionality is limited to materializations on the main branch only.
- [](#a855303b0205a22e2e9670b3fb405f87219417c938e65c6294dbe1d5835dbb4e)[Ontology / Ontology Management](/docs/foundry/ontology-manager/)Ontology Manager now displays which link type constraints are inherited when working with interfaces that extend other interfaces. This information is visible both on the **Extensions** tab and when previewing a new extension, making it easier to understand inheritance relationships between interfaces.
- [](#32021749c6bcc3fa0c4105b2058008596a681aadcb23a03812bee00043ac2e2b)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)You can now search for Gaia maps directly in the left search panel of Workflow Lineage. Previously, Gaia map nodes could only be accessed by expanding from existing nodes on the graph. This enhancement makes it easier to find and incorporate Gaia maps into your workflow visualizations.


**Note:** To search for Gaia maps in Workflow Lineage, your enrollment must use both Foundry and Gotham.

![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-02-18-13-57-18-gaia-map-nodes.png](2026-02-18-13-57-18-gaia-map-nodes.png)
- [](#b9c389d1d22e757a859b5e8c978fe53e042add18a2b3bf4cc3e32490ec532b24)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now provides more comprehensive information in the interface details panel. When viewing an interface, you can now see its properties, the object types that implement it, and the interfaces it extends from. This additional context makes it easier to understand interface relationships and structure within your ontology.

![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-02-13-10-46-45-interface-details.png](2026-02-13-10-46-45-interface-details.png)

## [](#February%2019,%202026)February 19, 20262026年2月19日

### [](#February%2019,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#d1fc78b9-0d5d-42b9-9c54-1f7f17bf3a34)[Ontology / Object Views](/docs/foundry/object-views/)Foundry now automatically creates a core [Object View](/docs/foundry/object-views/overview/) for a new object type to provide a standardized representation of all its objects, ensuring other users have a holistic understanding of its schema and links without requiring additional configuration. Core Object Views provide a consistent, complete display of object data after object type creation, and they are now generally available across Foundry enrollments. [Learn more about core Object Views](/docs/foundry/object-views/core-object-views/).

![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-02-18-175315-object-views-image-pn.png](2026-02-18-175315-object-views-image-pn.png)

- [](#e24940f3-7616-447c-9064-9a48e73b7ce6)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)You can now view execution and p95 metrics for your Logic functions directly in Workflow Lineage in the bottom **Function metrics** panel.

## [](#February%2012,%202026)February 12, 20262026年2月12日

### [](#February%2012,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#5fe5ea93-63ca-40d3-ae35-b6c86b395044)Ontology / IndexingDataset materializations are now supported for object types with row-level policies on organizations. This applies for restricted views and object security policies that reference a mandatory control property with a set of allowed organizations.

## [](#February%2011,%202026)February 11, 20262026年2月11日

### [](#February%2011,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#802d3506297b500ee864f88ae3a229626a3a36f47ee619be255717389cf1b1b3)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now supports geospatial map nodes in workflow visualizations. You can access these nodes through new connection buttons from other nodes, such as object types. This allows you to incorporate geospatial data into your ontology visualizations and better understand relationships between geospatial resources and other ontological elements.

### [](#February%2011,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#80e15e653af42305b6974e4d6a3673f12e982b68ef24ba7ec5312514a7c1908e)[Ontology / Automate](/docs/foundry/automate/)You can now open Workflow Lineage from an automation through an action button on the overview page or by using the `cmd+i` (macOS) or `ctrl+i` (Windows) keyboard shortcut.
- [](#91bdc2afe2bc337dc9b2ad3694a43a5195eb98b770b38e60394f26555623ca4c)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now automatically displays upstream and downstream nodes when opening a single item. Previously, when opening an Object Type, Action Type, Function, or Logic Function from Ontology Manager, only the selected node would appear in the graph. With this improvement, related nodes are immediately visible, providing better context and reducing the need for manual exploration.

## [](#February%2010,%202026)February 10, 20262026年2月10日

Use the presentation mode for Workflow Lineage to create and organize visual frames of your workflow graph, making it easier to present your work. To get started, select the project screen icon in the bottom of the graph.

## [](#February%204,%202026)February 4, 20262026年2月4日

### [](#February%204,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#485a1a315697f402da278237fc6c994c5713102d0190f4a03c163547b0758d27)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now distinguishes between link types that will be affected by permission changes and those that will not when using the permissions editing dialog. When editing object type permissions, the dialog separates link types into those that will have their permissions updated (based on your edit permissions) and those that will remain unaffected. This makes it clearer which ontological resources will have their permissions changed when using the bulk role updater.
- [](#626f930cc0871cf2d5104494a160072985dbd8e27fee629606458b107e0bf0b8)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now allows you to hide individual frames in presentation mode without deleting them. Hidden frames can be restored later when needed, giving you more flexibility in how you organize and present your workflow visualizations. Navigation buttons automatically disable when all frames in a particular direction are hidden, providing clear visual feedback about available navigation options.
- [](#e36bdfe516396fe29b1f8f45c801a8313a1271a7c36e7f0de57c28ba25eb1b5b)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now provides a more comprehensive visualization when opening interfaces from Ontology Manager. Instead of displaying object types that implement the interface in a simple grid layout, the system now creates a full dynamic layout showing richer relationships. This enhanced view includes interfaces the chosen interface extends, interfaces that extend it, and object types and interfaces referenced in link type constraints, giving you a more complete picture of your interface relationships.

![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-02-05-18-42-05-interface-example.png](2026-02-05-18-42-05-interface-example.png)

### [](#February%204,%202026-Fixes)Fixes修复

- [](#8097b0391e9b3f83b3b18ff7790598563ea4263eac976dd8ad1d7aef51c301fb)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now correctly preserves your latest auto-saved changes when resolving auto-save conflicts. Previously, choosing to abandon changes during an auto-save conflict would revert to the last manually saved state, potentially losing significant work. Now, the system reloads to the most recent auto-saved version, ensuring your latest changes are retained.

Instantly identify cross-ontology relationships, spot external resources at a glance, and switch between ontologies without leaving your workflow view.

## [](#January%2029,%202026)January 29, 20262026年1月29日

### [](#January%2029,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#2fa6dd90-599f-4eec-8729-32eeeaa4fe5c)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now includes a **Function metrics** tab that provides performance insights for your workflow functions and actions. The **P95 duration** sub-tab displays execution duration at the 95th percentile with intuitive graphs, allowing you to instantly spot performance spikes and proactively address potential issues. The **Executions** sub-tab shows the number of successful and failed executions for functions and actions, helping you identify reliability trends and troubleshoot issues more efficiently. These new metrics provide powerful insights, making it easier to monitor and optimize workflow functions.

本体论 / 工作流程 Lineage 现在包含一个功能指标标签页，提供工作流功能和动作的性能洞察。P95 持续时间子标签页将执行时长显示在第 95 百分位，并配有直观的图表，让你能够即时发现性能峰值，并主动解决潜在问题。执行子标签页显示功能和动作的成功和失败执行次数，帮助你识别可靠性趋势并更高效地排查问题。这些新指标提供了强大的洞察，使得监控和优化工作流程功能变得更容易。![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-28-10-00-33-workflow-lineage-chart.png](2026-01-28-10-00-33-workflow-lineage-chart.png)
- [](#83fc6d17-43a8-4f5b-aa87-360fadb172b0)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)You can now [filter run history](/docs/aip-observability/run-history/#filter-run-history) in Workflow Lineage to quickly find specific executions of functions, actions, automations, and logic. The **Run history** tab provides a complete view of all executions over the past seven days, and filtering by multiple criteria makes it faster to debug issues or audit workflows in high-volume environments.

本体论 / 工作流程谱系 你现在可以在工作流谱系中筛选运行历史，快速查找具体的函数、动作、自动化和逻辑执行。运行历史标签提供过去七天内所有执行的完整视图，并通过多重筛选方式加快了在高流量环境中调试问题或审计工作流程的速度。![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-28-165037-workflow-lineage-screenshot-2026-01-22-at-10-28-16-pn.png](2026-01-28-165037-workflow-lineage-screenshot-2026-01-22-at-10-28-16-pn.png)

![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-28-165040-workflow-lineage-screenshot-2026-01-22-at-10-30-56-pn.png](2026-01-28-165040-workflow-lineage-screenshot-2026-01-22-at-10-30-56-pn.png)

## [](#January%2027,%202026)January 27, 20262026年1月27日

### [](#January%2027,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#efa49ddc7be7b6476e5130e49cbc4b149fcef26c407f52098cb6de72722772e1)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Users can now view quiver dashboards as nodes in Workflow Lineage graphs. Quiver dashboard nodes function the same as other resource nodes, and have connections to the object types they use and the workshop modules they appear in. Different color modes can be used to view usage metrics, resource permissions, last modified dates, and more.

本体论 / 工作流程血脉用户现在可以在工作流血脉图中将箭袋仪表盘作为节点查看。Quiver 仪表盘节点的功能与其他资源节点相同，并且与它们使用的对象类型和出现的研讨会模块有连接。可以使用不同的颜色模式来查看使用指标、资源权限、最后修改日期等。![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-23-16-55-14-quiver-screenshot.png](2026-01-23-16-55-14-quiver-screenshot.png)

## [](#January%2026,%202026)January 26, 20262026年1月26日

### [](#January%2026,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#cfaf0669-2f78-4af0-b212-eccc1f0d5be1)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)Workflow Lineage now includes a new Action Rule color mode that visually distinguishes between different types of actions in your workflow. This color-coding system instantly shows whether an action runs a function, creates, modifies, or deletes an object. When used alongside the Action Rule histogram, you can quickly get a comprehensive overview of rule actions across your entire graph and filter actions within your current selection, making it easier to understand and manage complex workflows.

本体论 / 工作流程 Lineage 现在新增了一种新的动作规则颜色模式，可以直观区分工作流程中不同类型的动作。这种颜色编码系统能即时显示动作是否运行函数、创建、修改或删除对象。当与动作规则直方图配合使用时，你可以快速全面了解整个图表中的规则动作，并在当前选择中筛选动作，从而更容易理解和管理复杂的工作流程。![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-20-18-38-16-action-rule.png](2026-01-20-18-38-16-action-rule.png)

### [](#January%2026,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#091e4897-9036-461d-9aa5-5a6ac51cd6a0)[Ontology / Actions](/docs/foundry/action-types/)Near real-time metrics for functions and actions are now retained for 30 days instead of 7 days. This extended retention period allows you to observe longer-term performance trends and conduct more comprehensive analysis of your functions and actions over time.

本体论 / 动作 函数和动作的近实时指标现在保留30天，而非7天。这段延长的保留期让你能够观察更长期的绩效趋势，并对职能和行动进行更全面的分析。![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-22-10-04-30-actions-retention-30-days.png](2026-01-22-10-04-30-actions-retention-30-days.png)

## [](#January%2022,%202026)January 22, 20262026年1月22日

### [](#January%2022,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#ab90a58ea2395fa2080b447e1a4d2b016f61ea5fe150033340f53a76d04453df)[Ontology / Ontology Management](/docs/foundry/ontology-manager/)Managing data access and compliance for media sets often requires precise control over how markings are inherited and applied across your ontology. Configurable markings for media reference properties in Ontology Manager are now available on all Foundry enrollments. This capability allows you to define which markings are inherited per media source when configuring media reference properties.

本体论 / 本体管理管理媒体集的数据访问和合规性通常需要精确控制标记如何在本体中继承和应用。Ontology Manager 中媒体引用属性的可配置标记现已适用于所有 Foundry 注册。此功能允许您在配置媒体参考属性时，定义每个媒体源继承的标记。![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-16-150704-ontology-management-image-pn.png](2026-01-16-150704-ontology-management-image-pn.png)

### [](#January%2022,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#738b7f43-7edb-4007-a8c2-2df448956ff0)[Ontology / Automate](/docs/foundry/automate/)The Automate documentation has been restructured to improve discoverability. Updates include explanations of new features with current interface screenshots, expanded guidance for project and global scope modes, clarified limitations for automation dependencies, and a new workflow for backfilling large object sets using function-backed batches. Access the [full documentation](/docs/foundry/automate/overview/).

本体论  /  自动化自动化文档已被重组以提升可发现性。更新内容包括新功能解释及当前界面截图、扩展的项目和全局范围模式指南、澄清自动化依赖的限制，以及使用函数支持批处理大型对象集回填的新工作流程。 访问完整文档 。

## [](#January%2018,%202026)January 18, 20262026年1月18日

### [](#January%2018,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#97cd667cd24c22b0b7558603c07daa76e1e9acafb40e0a541e5b0e9883985b54)[Ontology / Object Views](/docs/foundry/object-views/)Object Views now work with Foundry Branching, allowing you to add, modify, and remove object views and their associated workshops directly on branches. You can rebase object views from the main branch, deploy changes to object views, and use modified object views from a branch within applications such as Workshop.

本体论  /  对象视图对象视图现在支持 Foundry Branching，允许你直接在分支上添加、修改和移除对象视图及其相关的工作坊。你可以从主分支重基对象视图，部署对象视图的更改，并在应用如 Workshop 内使用分支修改过的对象视图。
- [](#81ec8dd8be864e2a388e5c337728b87792540053980a33246aadcdb1cb4933dd)[Ontology / Ontology Management](/docs/foundry/ontology-manager/)Ontology Manager now includes an Observability tab for object types and link types. This tab displays existing monitor rules applied to the resource or prompts you to set up monitor rules if none exist, making it easier to track and manage monitoring for your ontology resources.

本体 / 本体管理本体管理器现在包含了对象类型和链接类型的可观察性标签。该标签页显示已应用到资源的监控规则，或者如果没有监控规则，提示你设置监控规则，方便跟踪和管理本体资源的监控。

## [](#January%2014,%202026)January 14, 20262026年1月14日

### [](#January%2014,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#4c1f398219b1c6f56c656232c12865db342404e1594517f192979a8b1a960481)[Ontology / Workflow Lineage](/docs/foundry/workflow-lineage/)When selecting multiple nodes in Workflow Lineage, you can now filter by rule type in the details panel. The histogram view includes a new category that groups nodes based on their action rules (create object, run function, etc.), making it easier to identify and select specific types of actions in complex workflows.

本体论  /  工作流程血脉在工作流血脉中选择多个节点时，你可以在详情面板中按规则类型进行筛选。直方图视图新增了一个类别，根据节点的动作规则（创建对象、运行函数等）分组，便于在复杂工作流程中识别和选择特定类型的动作。

## [](#January%2012,%202026)January 12, 20262026年1月12日

### [](#January%2012,%202026-Features)Features特征

- [](#06a17b919022e6d562e3d18174d514ce8ad8c24bb980b673fc44e88ce13db384)[Ontology / Ontology Management](/docs/foundry/ontology-manager/)Ontology Manager now allows you to copy and paste parameter override configurations between parameters in action forms. You can copy overrides from one parameter and paste them to another parameter in the same or different action form. When pasting, known parameter IDs are automatically filled, while unknown parameter IDs prompt you to either map them to available parameters or discard those criteria.

本体 / 本体管理现在允许你在动作表单中复制粘贴参数覆盖配置。你可以从一个参数复制覆盖，然后粘贴到另一个参数上，使用相同或不同的动作表态。粘贴时，已知参数 ID 会自动填充，而未知参数 ID 则提示你将其映射到可用参数或丢弃这些条件。

### [](#January%2012,%202026-Enhancements)Enhancements增强功能

- [](#8b7cb7e1-7f60-4af4-bbb0-284fd1c3c59e)[Ontology / Ontology Management](/docs/foundry/ontology-manager/)Ontology Manager now allows you to set up and inspect monitoring rules directly for functions and actions. You can view active monitoring rule status and history for these resources, providing better visibility into their performance and reliability.

本体/本体管理 Ontology Manager 现在允许您直接设置和检查功能和动作的监控规则。您可以查看这些资源的活跃监控规则状态和历史，从而更好地了解其性能和可靠性。![/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-12-11-57-32-2026-01-12-11-01-41-oma-function-monitoring-rules.png](2026-01-12-11-57-32-2026-01-12-11-01-41-oma-function-monitoring-rules.png)

You're all caught up 🎉你都跟🎉上了

Core Object Views provide a consistent, complete display of object data after object type creation, and they are now generally available across Foundry enrollments.\n\n### Why does Foundry configure core Object Views after you create an object type?\n\nProviding a default Object View that displays an object's prominent and standard properties saves Ontology builders time while ensuring other users gain maximum value from their interaction with the automatically created core representation. With Foundry handling the core Object View's creation, builders gain back time to create their own workflow-specific [custom Object Views](../object-views/config-overview.md) configured for a wider range of use cases, as needed. [Learn more about building custom Object Views using Foundry Branching](../object-views/branching-object-views.md).\n\n![A core Object View displays prominent and standard object properties as well as linked objects.](./media/2026-02-18-175315-object-views-image-pn.png)\n\n _A core Object View displays prominent and standard object properties as well as linked objects._\n\n### View prominent properties in base type-specific components\n\nFoundry surfaces [prominent properties](../object-link-types/property-metadata.md#metadata-reference) at the top of the core Object View to provide immediate context about an object's most important information.\n\nProperties marked as prominent receive enhanced visual treatment based on their type:\n\n* [Media reference properties](../object-link-types/base-types.md#media-references) render in a dedicated media viewer.\n* [Time series properties](../time-series/time-series-properties.md) display as interactive [Quiver](../quiver/overview.md) charts showing temporal data patterns.\n* [Geospatial properties](../geospatial/types-of-geospatial-and-geotemporal-data.md) automatically render on a [Foundry map](../map/overview.md).\n\nAll other prominent properties are displayed using a larger, card-style format elevated above a table displaying the remaining standard properties.\n\n![A core Object View displays prominent properties using different components derived from their base type.](./media/2026-02-18-175320-object-views-2026-02-02_21-08-34-2-gi.gif)\n\n_A core Object View displays prominent properties using different components derived from their base type._\n\n### View linked object types\n\nThe **Linked objects** component enables you to traverse between related objects directly within the core Object View. You can view linked objects grouped by link type, preview properties inline, and open linked objects in the side panel for further exploration.\n\n![The Linked objects component displays related objects grouped by their link type.](./media/2026-02-18-175324-object-views-linked-objects-component-pn.png)\n\n_The_ ***Linked objects*** _component displays related objects grouped by their link type._\n\nCore Object Views exist alongside [custom Object Views](../object-views/config-overview.md) built in [Workshop](../workshop/overview.md). While core Object Views display by default when no custom Object View is configured, they remain accessible even after you or another user build a custom Object View. You can toggle between core and custom Object Views at any time based on your specific workflow needs.\n\n![You can switch between core and custom Object Views using the view toggle.](./media/2026-02-18-175328-object-views-object-view-mode-switching-full-pn.png)\n\n_You can switch between core and custom Object Views using the view toggle._\n\nYou can view a core Object View.](./media/2026-02-18-175332-object-views-core-object-view-panel-pn.png)\n\n_The_ ***Linked objects*** _component is available in the panel form factor of an Object View._\n\nLearn more about how This follows a successful public beta period that started in October 2025.\n\nModel Studio transforms the complex task of building production-grade models into a streamlined no-code process that makes advanced machine learning more accessible. Whether you are a data scientist looking to accelerate your workflow, or a business user eager to unlock insights from your data, Model Studio provides essential tools and a user-friendly interface that simplifies the journey from data to model.\n\n![The Model Studio application home page displaying recent training runs and run details.](./media/2026-02-09-174447-model-studio-model_studio-pn.png)\n\n_The Model Studio application home page, displaying recent training runs and run details._\n\n### What is Model Studio?\n\nModel Studio is a no-code model development tool that allows you to train models in tasks such as forecasting, classification, and regression. With Model Studio, you can maximize model performance for your use cases by training models with custom data while retaining customization and control over the training process with optional parameter configuration.\n\nBuilding useful, production-ready models traditionally requires deep technical expertise and significant time investment, but Model Studio changes that by providing the following features:\n\n* **A streamlined point-and-click interface** for configuring model training jobs; no coding required.\n* **Built-in production-grade model trainers** tailored for common use cases such as time series forecasting, regression, and classification.\n* **Smart defaults and guided workflows** that empower you to get started quickly, even if you are new to machine learning.\n* **In-depth experiment tracking** with integrated performance metrics that allow you to monitor and refine your models with confidence.\n* **Full data lineage and secure access controls** built on top of the Palantir platform, ensuring transparency and security at every step.\n\n### Who should use Model Studio?\n\nModel Studio is perfect for technical and non-technical users alike. Business users who want to leverage machine learning without coding and data scientists who want to accelerate prototyping and model deployment can both benefit from Model Studio's tools and simplified process. Additionally, organizations can benefit from Model Studio by lowering the barrier to AI adoption and empowering more teams to build and use models.\n\n### Getting started\n\nTo get started with model training, open the Model Studio application and follow these steps:\n\n* Select the best model trainer for your use case (time series forecasting, classification, or regression).\n* Choose your input datasets.\n* Configure your model using intuitive options, or stick with the recommended defaults. \n\nAfter configuring your model, you can launch a training run and review model performance in real time with clear metrics and experiment tracking.\n\n### What's next on the development roadmap?\n\nAs Model Studio continues to evolve, we are committed to enhancing the user experience. To do so, we will introduce features such as:\n\n* Enhanced experiment logging for deeper training performance insights, including AI-readable content.\n* An expanded set of supported modeling tasks.\n* Full marketplace support for models built in Model Studio.\n* Direct support for time series inputs on top of datasets.\n\n[Learn more about Model Studio.](../model-studio/overview.md)\n\n### Tell us what you think\n\nAs we continue to develop Model Studio, we want to hear about your experiences and welcome your feedback. As a result of this improvement, we have deprecated standalone OAuth clients.\n\n### How to make your application unscoped\n\nAll Developer Console applications are created scoped by default. With compute modules, you can run containers that scale dynamically based on load, bringing your existing code, in any language, into Foundry without rewriting it.\n\n### What you can build\n\nCompute modules enable several key workflows in Foundry:\n\n**Custom functions and APIs**: Create functions that can be called from Workshop, Slate, Ontology SDK applications, and other Foundry environments. Host custom or open-source models from platforms like Hugging Face and query them directly from your applications.\n\n**Data pipelines**: Connect to external data sources and ingest data into Foundry streams, datasets, or media sets in real time. Use your own transformation logic to process data before writing it to outputs.\n\n**Legacy code integration**: Bring business-critical code written in any language into Foundry without translation. Use this code to back pipelines, Workshop modules, AIP Logic functions, or custom Ontology SDK applications.\n\n\n![An example of a compute module overview in Foundry with information about the job status functions and container metadeta.](./media/2026-02-04-170659-compute-modules-screenshot-2026-01-28-at-2-24-13-pm-pn.png)\n\n_An example of a compute module overview in Foundry, with information about the job status, functions, and container metadeta._\n\n### Why it matters\n\nCompute modules solve the challenge of integrating existing code into Foundry. Instead of rewriting your logic in a Foundry-supported language, containerize it and deploy it directly. The platform handles scaling, authentication, and connections to other Foundry resources automatically.\n\nKey features include:\n\n* Dynamic horizontal scaling based on current and predicted load\n* Zero-downtime updates when deploying new container versions\n* Native connections to Foundry datasets, Ontology resources, and APIs\n* External connections using REST, WebSockets, SSE, or other protocols\n* Marketplace compatibility for sharing modules across organizations\n\n### Get started\n\nReview the [compute modules documentation](../compute-modules/get-started.md) to build your first function or pipeline.\n\n\n\n","applications":[{"productId":"Foundry","categoryId":"dev-toolchain","categoryTitle":"Developer Toolchain","applicationTitle":"Compute Modules","frontendApplicationId":"compute-module-app","isKeyComponent":true}],"application":{"id":"","title":"Compute Modules"},"category":{"id":"dev-toolchain","title":"Developer Toolchain"},"product":{"id":"Foundry"}}],"date":"February 5, 2026"},{"id":"939604e2-45a6-4d9b-b428-04c013cde644","releaseNotes":[{"id":"3d6d4c8fd6812029eaf37ffcad7e78fc7d1f80474994ef3e9bc1903b1cf96683","type":"ENHANCEMENT","description":"AIP Evals now allows you to edit test case parameters directly from table column headers. AIP Document Intelligence is a low-code application for configuring and deploying document extraction workflows. Users can upload sample documents, experiment with different extraction strategies, and evaluate results based on quality, speed, and cost—all before deploying at scale. AIP Document Intelligence then generates Python transforms that can process entire document collections using the selected strategy, converting PDFs and images into structured Markdown with preserved tables and formatting.\n\n[Learn more about AIP Document Intelligence.](../document-intelligence/overview.md)\n\n![Result of Layout-aware OCR  Vision LLM extraction with metrics on cost speed and token usage.](./media/2026-02-03-152655-aip-document-intelligence-pasted_image-pn.png)\n\n_Result of Layout-aware OCR + Vision LLM extraction with metrics on cost, speed, and token usage._\n\n### Compare extraction strategies\n\nAIP Document Intelligence provides multiple extraction approaches, from traditional OCR to vision-language models. You can test each method on your specific documents and view side-by-side comparisons of extraction quality, processing time, and compute costs. This experimentation phase helps teams select the right approach for their use case without writing custom code.\n\n![Comparison of Vision LLM Extraction vs. Layout-aware OCR  Vision LLM Extraction shows drastic improvement in complex table extraction quality.](./media/2026-02-03-152701-aip-document-intelligence-image-pn.png)\n\n_Comparison of Vision LLM Extraction vs. Layout-aware OCR + Vision LLM Extraction shows drastic improvement in complex table extraction quality._\n\n### Deploy extraction pipelines in one click\n\nOnce a strategy is configured, AIP Document Intelligence generates production-ready Python transforms that process documents at scale. The latest deployment uses lightweight transforms rather than Spark, significantly improving processing speed. Workflows that previously took days extracting data from document collections can now complete the same work in hours. [Refer to the documentation](../document-intelligence/deploy-to-python-transforms.md) for more detailed instruction on how to deploy and customize your Python transforms.\n\n![Choose a validated extraction strategy and deploy to a Python transforms to batch process documents.](./media/2026-02-03-152705-aip-document-intelligence-screenshot-2026-01-30-at-11-04-05-am-pn.png)\n\n_Choose a validated extraction strategy and deploy to a Python transforms to batch process documents._\n\n### Maintain quality across diverse document types\n\nEnterprise documents vary widely in structure, formatting, and content density. AIP Document Intelligence handles this diversity through configurable extraction strategies that can adapt to multi-column layouts, embedded tables, and mixed-language content. Users working with maintenance manuals, regulatory filings, invoices have successfully extracted structured data while preserving critical formatting and relationships.\n\n### When to use AIP Document Intelligence\n\nAIP Document Intelligence is designed for workflows where document content needs to be extracted and structured for downstream AI applications. This includes:\n\n* **Populating vector databases** for retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems\n* **Extracting tabular data** from reports, invoices, or forms for analysis\n* **Converting legacy documentation** into searchable, structured formats\n* **Preparing training data** for domain-specific language models\n\nFor workflows that require extracting specific entities (like part numbers, dates, or named entities) rather than full document content, upcoming entity extraction capabilities will provide more targeted functionality.\n\n### What's next on the development roadmap?\n\n* **Entity extraction from documents:** The team is developing capabilities to extract structured entities, such as equipment identifiers, monetary values, dates, and custom domain concepts, directly from documents. This will enable direct population of Ontology objects from unstructured sources.\n* **Broader use of AIP Document Intelligence:** Allow extraction configurations to be called directly from AIP Logic and Ontology functions to expand Document Intelligence beyond Python transforms to broader workflow automation scenarios.\n\n### Your feedback matters\n\nWe want to hear about your experiences using AIP Document Intelligence and welcome your feedback. Branching enables safer iteration by allowing you to test changes in isolation, collaborate with multiple teams without conflicts, and ensure quality before deployment—using the same workflows you already use for Workshop modules and Ontology resources.\n\n**Key features:**\n\n* **Branch-based development:** Add, remove, and modify object views on branches to safely iterate on structural changes (tabs, visibility conditions) and content changes (Workshop modules) without affecting production.\n* **Cross-application testing:** Embed branched object views in Workshop applications and preview them in Ontology Manager to validate changes before merging.\n* **Conflict resolution:** Rebase your object views when changes occur on `main`, with an intuitive dialog that automatically resolves non-conflicting changes and guides you through resolving conflicts.\n\n![Example of object views and their associated modified Workshop modules on a Foundry branch. Here we have a single Object Type named Museum modified on the branch. The Full Object View Tabs resource represents structural changes to the object view itself. The Full Object View  Museum History and Panel Object View resources represent changes to Workshop modules used by the object view.](./media/2026-01-27-191757-foundry-branching-pasted_image-pn.png)\n\n_Example of object views and their associated (modified) Workshop modules on a Foundry branch. Here we have a single Object Type named \"Museum\" modified on the branch. The \"Full Object View Tabs\" resource represents structural changes to the object view itself. The \"Full Object View • Museum History\" and \"Panel Object View\" resources represent changes to Workshop modules used by the object view._\n\n![When conflicts are detected between your branch and main  you will be prompted to rebase and be shown this dialog to resolve any conflicts.](./media/2026-01-27-191801-foundry-branching-pasted_image-pn.png)\n\n_When conflicts are detected between your branch and_ `main` _, you will be prompted to rebase and be shown this dialog to resolve any conflicts._\n\nKnown limitations:\n\n* Approvals are not yet supported, so all object view changes on branches are automatically approved.\n* Legacy object view tabs cannot be edited on branches.\n\n### Getting started\n\nTo add an object view to a branch, save an object view version while on a branch in the Object View editor, accessed through the Ontology Manager. For detailed guidance on working with branched object views, refer to the [documentation](../object-views/branching-object-views.md).\n\n### What's next in the development roadmap?\n\nFull approvals integration with reviewers, policies, and resource protection on the `main` branch.","applications":[{"productId":"Foundry","categoryId":"dev-toolchain","categoryTitle":"Developer Toolchain","applicationId":"foundry-branching","applicationTitle":"Foundry Branching","frontendApplicationId":"developer-branching","isKeyComponent":true}],"application":{"id":"foundry-branching","title":"Foundry Branching"},"category":{"id":"dev-toolchain","title":"Developer Toolchain"},"product":{"id":"Foundry"}},{"id":"70f9a0b1-009a-40ad-8ae7-b4710db7d943","type":"FEATURE","description":"Products packaged in DevOps can now track a source folder. Instead of manually maintaining individual resources, DevOps will automatically include resources from the source folder every time you release a new version.\n\nTracking a source folder is useful for streamlining releases of new products when you have a well-defined project that reflects the resources you want to include in your product.\n\n![DevOps new product landing page now gives the option to track a source folder.](./media/2026-01-27-195707-devops-image-pn.png)\n\n_DevOps new product landing page now gives the option to track a source folder._\n\n### Configurations options\n\nFor files that are not present in the Compass filesystem, you can use folder settings to additionally track related resources. For example, you can track all health checks that exist on datasets in the folder or functions that are defined in Code Repositories in the folder. You can also exclude resources by configuring ignored sub-folders for outputs that should not be packaged, such as experimental work.\n\nFor added flexibility, you can combine both manually added outputs and folder tracked outputs. This allows you to manually add resources that do not exist within the Compass filesystem and are not covered by settings.\n\n![Several configuration settings are available when tracking a source folder.](./media/2026-01-27-195713-devops-image-pn.png)\n\n_Several configuration settings are available when tracking a source folder._\n\n### Migrate an existing product to track a source folder\n\nIf you have an existing product where resources were added manually, you can perform a one-time migration to configure your product to track a source folder, if your resources share a common Compass project. The migration dialog will show you a preview including resources that will now be tracked as part of the folder, as well as resources that will continue to be manually tracked because they are not within the Compass filesystem or brought in by folder tracking settings.\n\nIf you decide that folder tracking is no longer suitable for your product, you can switch back to manual output management using the **Disable folder** tracking option.\n\n![The folder tracking migration modal allows you to migrate existing products to track a source folder.](./media/2026-01-27-195720-devops-image-pn.png)\n\n_The folder tracking migration modal allows you to migrate existing products to track a source folder._\n\n[Learn more about tracking a source folder in DevOps.](../foundry-devops/folder-tracking.md)","applications":[{"productId":"Foundry","categoryId":"devops","categoryTitle":"DevOps","applicationTitle":"DevOps","frontendApplicationId":"marketplace-packaging-app","isKeyComponent":true}],"application":{"id":"","title":"DevOps"},"category":{"id":"devops","title":"DevOps"},"product":{"id":"Foundry"}},{"id":"2fa6dd90-599f-4eec-8729-32eeeaa4fe5c","type":"FEATURE","description":"Workflow Lineage now includes a **Function metrics** tab that provides performance insights for your workflow functions and actions. The **Run history** tab provides a complete view of all executions over the past seven days, and filtering by multiple criteria makes it faster to debug issues or audit workflows in high-volume environments.\n\n### Available filters\n\nFilter run history by any combination of the following criteria:\n\n* **Status**: Successful or failed executions\n* **Timestamp range**: Executions within a specified date range\n* **User**: Executions triggered by a specific user\n* **Run time range**: Executions within a specified duration range\n* **Version**: Executions for a specified version (functions only)\n* **Caller**: Executions originating from a specified resource\n* **Failure type**: Executions that failed for a specific reason\n\n![The run history for a function execution filtered by timestamp runtime and caller RID.](./media/2026-01-28-165037-workflow-lineage-screenshot-2026-01-22-at-10-28-16-pn.png)\n\n_The run history for a function execution filtered by timestamp, runtime, and caller RID._\n\n![The run history for a logic execution filtered by status and failure reason.](./media/2026-01-28-165040-workflow-lineage-screenshot-2026-01-22-at-10-30-56-pn.png)\n\n_The run history for a logic execution filtered by status and failure reason._\n\nWhen you specify multiple filters, results will include only executions that match all specified filters. For example, find failed executions triggered by a specific user within the last 24 hours, or identify long-running executions that exceeded a certain duration threshold.\n\nThis feature is available across all enrollments. Reserved capacity helps ensure uninterrupted operations by protecting critical production workflows from shared project or enrollment limits on tokens and requests.\n\n### What is reserved capacity?\n\nReserved capacity allows you to reserve dedicated tokens per minute (TPM) and requests per minute (RPM) on LLMs for critical production workflows, ensuring they are not impacted by shared project or enrollment limits. [Learn more about this feature in the documentation.](https://www.palantir.com/docs/foundry/aip/llm-capacity-management/#aip-reserved-capacity)\n\nThere is no additional cost to use reserved capacity. \n\n### How to view your reserved capacity\n\nTo view all reserved capacity offerings on an enrollment: \n\n* Navigate to **Resource Management \u003e AIP usage \u0026 limits \u003e Reserved capacity**.\n* Select the model from the dropdown to see available capacity.\n* If the **Reserved capacity** tab is not present, it means reserved capacity is not currently available for your environment.\n\n![You can view reserved capacity in Resource Management.](./media/2026-01-27-173339-language-model-service-image-pn.png)\n\n_You can view reserved capacity in Resource Management._\n\nWhen a project reaches its reserved capacity limit, that project will seamlessly continue operating by using the standard project and enrollment limits. Reserved capacity provides extra throughput on top of your existing limits and is available only for projects specifically enabled by an enrollment administrator.\n\n### Your feedback matters\n\nWe want to hear about your experiences using reserved capacity in the Palantir platform and welcome your feedback. Each space comes with a set of default roles and the ability to create custom roles for greater flexibility in managing permissions. For each role, you can open the workflows dropdown menu to view the permissions granted with the role. Select a role to view the role grants in the panel on the right, where you can add or remove users.\n\n\n![The Space permissions page in Control Panel showing the various workflows granted with the Contributor role.](./media/2026-01-14-143132-projects-space-permissions-pn.png)\n\n_The_ ***Space permissions*** _page in Control Panel, showing the various workflows granted with the `Contributor` role._\n\nTo create a custom role, select **+ New role** in the top right of the page, then select the workflows to include with this role. After creating the custom role, you can grant that role to users the same way you would for other roles. Custom roles can be edited or deleted through the **Actions** menu in the top right of each custom role.\n\n\nNote that custom roles are \"frozen\", meaning that new workflows added to default roles will not automatically apply to custom roles. To include new workflows in a custom role, select **Edit role** and add them manually.\n\nFor more information on space and organization management, [review our documentation](../platform-security-management/manage-orgs-and-spaces.md).\n\n","applications":[{"productId":"Foundry","categoryId":"security","categoryTitle":"Security","applicationId":"compass","applicationTitle":"Projects","frontendApplicationId":"compass","isKeyComponent":true}],"application":{"id":"compass","title":"Projects"},"category":{"id":"security","title":"Security"},"product":{"id":"Foundry"}},{"id":"a4fd9756-5507-49df-9557-bff183a08d28","type":"FEATURE","description":"All ontologies created after Wednesday, January 21, will use the project permissions system by default. With project-based permissions, the ability to view, edit, and manage ontology resources are managed through [Compass](/foundry/compass/overview/), the Palantir platform's filesystem. ","categoryTitle":"Security","categoryId":"security","applicationId":"compass","applicationTitle":"Projects","date":"January 15, 2026","title":"New ontologies will now use project permissions","prominence":"Announce","releaseVersion":"","productId":"Foundry","frontendApplicationId":"compass","mediaFilenames":["/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-14-183402-projects-screenshot-2026-01-12-at-12-54-29-pn.png"],"longDescription":"## New ontologies will now use project permissions\n\nAll ontologies created after Wednesday, January 21, will use the project permissions system by default. With project-based permissions, the ability to view, edit, and manage ontology resources is managed through [Compass](../compass/overview.md), the Palantir platform's filesystem. This is the same permissions system other resource types use. \n\nThis project-based permissions approach replaces the previous permission models: [ontology roles and datasource-derived permissions](../object-permissioning/ontology-permissions-legacy.md). \n\n### Key benefits of the project permissions system\n\nThe project-based permission model offers multiple benefits:\n\n* **Unified permission model:** Ontology resources now use the same permission system as other resource types, so you only need to learn and manage permissions in one place.\n* **Bulk management:** Set permissions at the folder or project level to control access across multiple resources at once, eliminating the need to set permissions on individual items.\n* **Clearer visibility:** The **Security** tab and sidebar now display permissions and project context for all resources, including ontologies.\n* **Increased functionality:** As project resources, ontologies gain access to Compass features like folders, access requests, markings, and tags.\n\nTo migrate existing Ontology resources to project-based permissions, review [migration guidance](../ontology-manager/migrate-to-project-based-permissions.md).\n\n### Opting out of this change\n\nTo continue the use of a legacy permissions system for new ontologies instead, navigate to the **Configuration** tab in **Ontology Manager** and turn off **New ontology resources will be saved in a project**. \n\n![To prevent newly-created ontologies from defaulting to the project-based permissions system, navigate to the Configuration tab in Ontology Manager and turn off the New ontology resources will be saved in a project setting.](./media/2026-01-14-183402-projects-screenshot-2026-01-12-at-12-54-29-pn.png)\n\n_To prevent newly-created ontologies from defaulting to the project-based permissions system, navigate to the_ ***Configuration*** _tab in_ ***Ontology Manager*** _and turn off the_ ***New ontology resources will be saved in a project*** _setting._\n\n### Current limitations\n\nProject permissions for the ontology are not available yet with classification-based access controls (CBAC) or default ontologies. \n\n### We want to hear from you\n\nWe hope these enhancements improve and simplify your permission workflows. Share your thoughts through Palantir Support channels or on our [Developer Community ↗](https://community.palantir.com/) or post using the [`Ontology management` tag Resources in your Developer Console application (including objects, actions, and queries) become tools that agents can discover and use. This works with pro-code frameworks (LangChain, CrewAI, custom Python/TypeScript) and low-code platforms (Copilot Studio, other agent builders). Ontology MCP will be available in beta for all users with Developer Console access by the end of January 2026.\n\n![The Ontology MCP configuration page in Developer Console with the Claude Code agent selected.](./media/2026-01-12-175733-ontology-mcp-ontology-mcp-pn.png)\n\n_The Ontology MCP configuration page in Developer Console with the Claude Code agent selected._\n\n### What's new?\n\nPreviously, connecting AI agents to the Ontology required building custom integrations for each source system and agent framework, requiring deep knowledge of both the framework's API patterns and Foundry's SDK. With Ontology MCP, you can configure your MCP server once and connect any compatible agent framework. The MCP protocol handles authentication, tool discovery, and execution. Your Developer Console application defines which resources agents can access, and MCP ensures agents can only interact with the resources you have explicitly exposed.\n\n### When to use Ontology MCP\n\n* You are building AI agents that need to interact with Ontology data or actions\n* You want to support multiple agent frameworks without maintaining separate integrations\n* You need to enable teams with different development preferences to access the same Ontology resources\n* You need fine-grained control over which Ontology resources agents can access\n\n### Getting started\n\nTo start using Ontology MCP, open your Developer Console application and navigate to the **MCP** tab on the left. Choose to **Enable MCP clients to connect to this application using MCP**, and add a Markdown-supported description for the MCP server. Then, select your agent framework from the list to view framework-specific installation instructions\n\n### Ontology MCP and AIP Agents\n\nOntology MCP extends Ontology access to external agent frameworks. [AIP Agents](../agent-studio/overview.md) provide native agent-building capabilities within the platform. Use AIP Agents for in-platform workflows and Ontology MCP when connecting external frameworks to your Ontology.\n\nFor more information about Ontology MCP and how to use agents in Foundry and your Developer Console applications, watch the [YouTube video ↗](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_-dzTtTFiqg) from our DevCon 4 presentation.\n\n","applications":[{"productId":"Foundry","categoryId":"dev-toolchain","categoryTitle":"Developer Toolchain","applicationTitle":"Ontology MCP","frontendApplicationId":"dev-console-app","isKeyComponent":true}],"application":{"id":"","title":"Ontology MCP"},"category":{"id":"dev-toolchain","title":"Developer Toolchain"},"product":{"id":"Foundry"}}],"date":"January 13, 2026"},{"id":"50ce98d0-de7e-48a3-a3d7-f0a31743dea3","releaseNotes":[{"id":"183d086bfd90d138eac44a5acb77de95677f198264f7be2659934adff6dadf22","type":"FIX","description":"Workshop now allows users to create boolean arrays with static values in variable transformations. [Learn more from the documentation on Listeners](/foundry/data-connection/listeners-overview/).","categoryTitle":"Data Integration","categoryId":"data-integration","applicationId":"data-connection","applicationTitle":"Data Connection","date":"January 8, 2026","title":"Introducing listeners in Data Connection for capturing inbound webhooks","prominence":"Announce","releaseVersion":"","productId":"Foundry","frontendApplicationId":"data-ingestion-app","mediaFilenames":["/docs/resources/foundry/announcements/release-notes/2026-01-07-212444-data-connection-image-pn.png"],"longDescription":"## Introducing listeners in Data Connection for capturing inbound webhooks\n\nListeners, a new Data Connection feature, enables you to receive inbound webhook events directly into the Palantir platform. This feature will be released in public beta the week of January 5th. Integrating real-time events from external systems into Foundry has traditionally been challenging when those systems lack OAuth 2.0 authentication support or cannot format payloads to match standard Foundry API endpoints. Listeners address this gap by provisioning URL endpoints that implement system-specific message signing and verification schemes—agnostic to data shape—providing a simple, low-latency mechanism to accept event streams from external sources.\n\n[For more information, including a list of supported listeners and set up guides, review the Listeners documentation.](../data-connection/listeners-overview.md)\n\n![Select from Data Connections supported listeners to configure and receive inbound webhook events.](./media/2026-01-07-212444-data-connection-image-pn.png)\n\n_Select from Data Connection's supported listeners to configure and receive inbound webhook events._\n\n### How listeners work\n\nTo accept inbound events from external systems, Data Connection listeners provision a URL endpoint, implement the specific message signing or other verification schemes for specific external systems, and allow a simple and low-latency mechanism to receive event streams into the Palantir platform. Leverage the listener output stream with streaming pipelines, automations, or batch analysis to create powerful event-processing workflows.\n\n### Subdomain configuration and zero-downtime endpoint rotation \n\nYou can generate a subdomain for your listener to establish a distinct ingress point with a wider range of network ingress compared to the rest of your Foundry enrollment. This isolates webhook traffic from other platform operations, provides additional control over external system connections, and enables unified governance with additional security benefits.\n\nListeners also come with an endpoint rotation capability that provides protection if a listener endpoint is compromised. Migrate to a new endpoint with zero downtime if the URL is accidentally exposed. When rotating your endpoint, you can set an expiration date for seamless zero-downtime transitions, or delete the old endpoint immediately if faster action is required. Once an endpoint expires, it will no longer process events.\n\nData Connection listeners expand Foundry's integration capabilities by removing authentication and payload formatting barriers that previously prevented real-time event ingestion from external systems.\n\n[For more information, see the listener subdomains documentation.](../data-connection/listeners-subdomains.md)\n\n### Get started with listeners\n\nEnrollment administrators can enable listeners by toggling the feature on in the **Data Connection** page under **Control Panel**. \n\nOnce enabled, users can access the **Listeners** tab from within the Data Connection application to connect the Palantir platform to external systems and workflows.\n\n### Supported listeners\n\nThe Palantir platform currently provides support for the following listeners:\n\n * [AWS SNS ↗](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/sns/latest/dg/sns-http-https-endpoint-as-subscriber.html)\n * [Azure Event Hub [Jira Automation ↗](https://support.atlassian.com/cloud-automation/docs/jira-cloud-automation/)\n * [Jotform ↗](https://www.jotform.com/integrations/webhooks)\n * [Microsoft Bot Framework ## Do Not Sell or Share My Personal Data

Your Opt Out Preference Signal is Honored- ### Your Privacy
- ### Strictly Necessary Cookies
- ### Share Or Sale of Personal Data

#### Your Privacy

When you visit our website, we store cookies on your browser to collect information. The information collected might relate to you, your preferences or your device, and is mostly used to make the site work as you expect it to and to provide a more personalized web experience. However, you can choose not to allow certain types of cookies, which may impact your experience of the site and the services we are able to offer. Click on the different category headings to find out more and change our default settings according to your preference. You cannot opt-out of our First Party Strictly Necessary Cookies as they are deployed in order to ensure the proper functioning of our website (such as prompting the cookie banner and remembering your settings, to log into your account, to redirect you when you log out, etc.). For more information about the First and Third Party Cookies used please follow this link.
            
[More information](https://www.palantir.com/cookie-statement/)

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always ActiveThese cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

Cookies Details‎#### Share Or Sale of Personal Data

  Share Or Sale of Personal Data Under the CPRA, you have the right to opt-out of the sale or sharing of your personal information to third parties. These cookies collect information for analytics and to personalize your experience with targeted ads. You may exercise your right to opt out of the sale or sharing of personal information by using this toggle switch. If you opt out we will not be able to offer you personalized ads and will not hand over your personal information to any third parties. Additionally, you may contact our legal department for further clarification about your rights as a California consumer by using this Exercise My Rights link.If you have enabled privacy controls on your browser (such as a plugin), we have to take that as a valid request to opt-out. Therefore we would not be able to track your activity through the web. This may affect our ability to personalize ads according to your preferences.

- ##### Targeting Cookies

  Switch Label labelThese cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.
